 üß™ –ü—Ä–∏—ë–º–∫–∞

      desc: ` üéØ –¶–µ–ª—å

–°–æ–∑–¥–∞—Ç—å –∞–≥–µ–Ω—Ç–∞, –∫–æ—Ç–æ—Ä—ã–π –ø–æ —Å–æ–¥–µ—Ä–∂–∞–Ω–∏—é –ª–µ–Ω–¥–∏–Ω–≥–∞ –ø—Ä–µ–¥–ª–∞–≥–∞–µ—Ç —Ä–µ–∫–æ–º–µ–Ω–¥–∞—Ü–∏–∏ –ø–æ —É–ª—É—á—à–µ–Ω–∏—é —Å—Ç—Ä—É–∫—Ç—É—Ä—ã –∏ –≤–∏–∑—É–∞–ª—å–Ω–æ–π –ø–æ–¥–∞—á–∏.

‚öôÔ∏è –õ–æ–≥–∏–∫–∞ —Ä–∞–±–æ—Ç—ã

1\. –ó–∞–≥—Ä—É–∂–∞–µ—Ç HTML –ø–æ —Å—Å—ã–ª–∫–µ, –∏–∑–≤–ª–µ–∫–∞–µ—Ç —Ç–µ–∫—Å—Ç.  
2\. –ü—Ä–æ–º–ø—Ç: ¬´–¢—ã UI-–¥–∏–∑–∞–π–Ω–µ—Ä. –î–∞–π —Å–æ–≤–µ—Ç—ã –ø–æ —É–ª—É—á—à–µ–Ω–∏—é —Å—Ç—Ä—É–∫—Ç—É—Ä—ã –∏ –¥–∏–∑–∞–π–Ω–∞ —ç—Ç–æ–≥–æ –ª–µ–Ω–¥–∏–Ω–≥–∞.¬ª

‚úÖ –§—É–Ω–∫—Ü–∏–æ–Ω–∞–ª—å–Ω—ã–µ —Ç—Ä–µ–±–æ–≤–∞–Ω–∏—è

\- –û–±—Ä–∞–±–æ—Ç–∫–∞ —Å–±–æ–µ–≤ –∏ –ª–æ–≥–∏—Ä–æ–≤–∞–Ω–∏–µ.

üõ° –ù–µ—Ñ—É–Ω–∫—Ü–∏–æ–Ω–∞–ª—å–Ω—ã–µ —Ç—Ä–µ–±–æ–≤–∞–Ω–∏—è

\- Python ‚â• 3.10, —Å —Ç–∏–ø–∞–º–∏ –∏ PEP8.  
\- –•—Ä–∞–Ω–µ–Ω–∏–µ –∫–ª—é—á–µ–π ‚Äî —á–µ—Ä–µ–∑ \`.env\`.

landing_redesign_assistant/
‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ agent.py
‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ openai_module.py
‚îú‚îÄ‚îÄ requirements.txt
‚îî‚îÄ‚îÄ README.md

üß™ –ü—Ä–∏—ë–º–∫–∞

\- –ü—Ä–µ–¥–ª–æ–∂–µ–Ω–∏—è –∫–æ–Ω—Å—Ç—Ä—É–∫—Ç–∏–≤–Ω—ã –∏ –æ–±–æ—Å–Ω–æ–≤–∞–Ω—ã.  
\- –í—Å–µ —Ä–µ–∫–æ–º–µ–Ω–¥–∞—Ü–∏–∏ —Å–æ–æ—Ç–≤–µ—Ç—Å—Ç–≤—É—é—Ç —Å–æ–¥–µ—Ä–∂–∞–Ω–∏—é —Å—Ç—Ä–∞–Ω–∏—Ü—ã.  
\- –†–∞–±–æ—Ç–∞ —É—Å—Ç–æ–π—á–∏–≤–∞ –∫ —Å–±–æ—è–º.
`
  }
    /* ‚Äî –¥–æ–±–∞–≤—å—Ç–µ –æ—Å—Ç–∞–ª—å–Ω—ã–µ –ø—Ä–æ–µ–∫—Ç—ã –¥–æ 30 ‚Äî */
  ];

  /* 4. –°–æ—Å—Ç–æ—è–Ω–∏–µ */
  let attempts = Number(localStorage.getItem(ATTEMPT_KEY)) || 0;
  let history  = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem(HISTORY_KEY) || '[]');
  let used     = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem(USED_KEY)    || '[]');
  const savedChoice = localStorage.getItem(CHOICE_KEY);
  const alreadySaved = localStorage.getItem(SAVED_KEY) === '1';

  if (savedChoice) resultBox.innerHTML = savedChoice;
  btnSave.disabled = !savedChoice || alreadySaved;
  if (alreadySaved) btnSave.textContent = '‚úì –°–æ—Ö—Ä–∞–Ω–µ–Ω–æ';

  renderHistory();
  updateUI();

  /* 5. –ü–æ–ª—É—á–∏—Ç—å / –ü–æ–º–µ–Ω—è—Ç—å */
  btnRoll.addEventListener('click', () => {
    if (attempts >= MAX_ATTEMPTS) return;

    const available = projects
      .map((p,i)=>({...p, idx:i}))
      .filter(p => !used.includes(p.idx));

    if (!available.length) return;

    const pick = available[Math.floor(Math.random()*available.length)];
    const html = formatProject(pick);

    resultBox.innerHTML = html;
    btnSave.disabled = false;
    btnSave.textContent = '–°–æ—Ö—Ä–∞–Ω–∏—Ç—å';
    localStorage.removeItem(SAVED_KEY);          // —Å–±—Ä–æ—Å–∏–ª–∏ –º–µ—Ç–∫—É

    used.push(pick.idx);
    history.push(html);

    localStorage.setItem(CHOICE_KEY,  html);
    localStorage.setItem(USED_KEY,    JSON.stringify(used));
    localStorage.setItem(HISTORY_KEY, JSON.stringify(history));
    localStorage.setItem(ATTEMPT_KEY, ++attempts);

    renderHistory();
    updateUI();
  });

  /* 6. –ò—Å—Ç–æ—Ä–∏—è */
  btnHist.addEventListener('click', () => {
    histWrap.style.display = histWrap.style.display === 'none' ? 'block' : 'none';
  });

  /* 7. –°–æ—Ö—Ä–∞–Ω–∏—Ç—å */
  btnSave.addEventListener('click', async () => {
    if (btnSave.disabled) return;
    const title = resultBox.querySelector('.proj-title')?.textContent || '';
    if (!title) return;

    const desc = resultBox.innerText.replace(title,'').trim();

    const payload = {
      lesson_id     : LESSON_ID,
      user_id       : USER_ID,
      project_title : title,
      project_desc  : desc,
      attempts_left : MAX_ATTEMPTS - attempts,
      timestamp     : new Date().toISOString()
    };

    try {
      if (USE_GET) {
        const qs = new URLSearchParams(payload).toString();
        await fetch(`${SAVE_ENDPOINT}?${qs}`, { mode:'cors' });
      } else {
        await fetch(SAVE_ENDPOINT, {
          method  : 'POST',
          mode    : 'cors',
          headers : { 'Content-Type':'application/json' },
          body    : JSON.stringify(payload)
        });
      }
      btnSave.textContent = '‚úì –°–æ—Ö—Ä–∞–Ω–µ–Ω–æ';
      btnSave.disabled = true;
      localStorage.setItem(SAVED_KEY, '1');     // –ø–æ–º–µ—Ç–∏–ª–∏ ¬´—É–∂–µ –æ—Ç–ø—Ä–∞–≤–ª–µ–Ω–æ¬ª
    } catch (err) {
      console.error(err);
      btnSave.textContent = '–û—à–∏–±–∫–∞';
    }
  });

  /* 8. –í—Å–ø–æ–º–æ–≥–∞—Ç–µ–ª—å–Ω—ã–µ —Ñ—É–Ω–∫—Ü–∏–∏ */
  function updateUI(){
    const left = MAX_ATTEMPTS - attempts;
    hint.textContent   = left>0 ? `–û—Å—Ç–∞–ª–æ—Å—å –ø–æ–ø—ã—Ç–æ–∫: ${left}` : '–ü–æ–ø—ã—Ç–∫–∏ –∑–∞–∫–æ–Ω—á–∏–ª–∏—Å—å.';
    btnRoll.disabled   = left===0;
    btnRoll.textContent= attempts===0 ? '–ü–æ–ª—É—á–∏—Ç—å –ø—Ä–æ–µ–∫—Ç' : '–ü–æ–º–µ–Ω—è—Ç—å';
    btnHist.disabled   = history.length===0;
  }

  function renderHistory(){
    histList.innerHTML = history.map((item,i)=>`
      <div class="history-item">
        <div style="font-weight:500;margin-bottom:8px;">#${i+1}</div>
        ${item}
        <button class="select-btn" data-idx="${i}">–í—ã–±—Ä–∞—Ç—å</button>
      </div>`
    ).join('<hr class="history-sep">');

    document.querySelectorAll('.select-btn').forEach(btn=>{
      btn.addEventListener('click',e=>{
        const idx  = +e.currentTarget.dataset.idx;
        const html = history[idx];
        resultBox.innerHTML = html;

        btnSave.disabled = false;
        btnSave.textContent = '–°–æ—Ö—Ä–∞–Ω–∏—Ç—å';
        localStorage.removeItem(SAVED_KEY);     // —Å–±—Ä–æ—Å–∏–ª–∏ —Ñ–ª–∞–≥

        localStorage.setItem(CHOICE_KEY, html);
      });
    });
  }

  function formatProject(p){
    return `<strong class="proj-title">${p.title}</strong><br>` +
           p.desc.replace(/\*\*(.+?)\*\*/g,'<strong>$1</strong>').replace(/\n/g,'<br>');
  }
})();
</script>
		</div>

</div></div>

	function setElementEvents() {
		if (!window.readyStatusSet) {
			window.readyStatusSet = true;
			$('.answer-form textarea').autosize();
			$('#lessonAnswerForm').submit(function () {
				$('.send-answer-value').attr('name', 'send-answer');
				$('.btn-send-answer, .btn-save-draft').attr('disabled', 'disabled');
				return true;
			});

			$('.btn-save-draft').on("click", function () {
				let isBeforeTestingStage = $('.before-start-block').first().length > 0;
				if (isBeforeTestingStage) {
					return false;
				}

				$('#lessonAnswerForm').append('<input type="hidden" name="is-draft" value="1" />');
				return true;
			});
		}
	}
	$(function () {
		setElementEvents();
	})

	function checkReady() {
		setElementEvents()
	}

	window.setTimeout(checkReady, 2000);
</script>

<script>
  window.addEventListener('message', function(event) {
    var data = event.data;
    if (data && data.key === 'YAUTM') {
      // –î–µ–ª–∞–µ–º —á—Ç–æ-—Ç–æ —Å –ø–æ–ª—É—á–µ–Ω–Ω—ã–º –∑–Ω–∞—á–µ–Ω–∏–µ–º
      let encodedCookieValue = data.value;
      document.cookie = `YA_ZEROCODER_UTM=${encodedCookieValue}; path=/; SameSite=None; Secure`;
    }
  });

  function getCookie(name) {
    var nameEQ = name + "=";
    var ca = document.cookie.split(';');
    for (var i = 0; i < ca.length; i++) {
      var c = ca[i];
      while (c.charAt(0) == ' ') c = c.substring(1, c.length);
      if (c.indexOf(nameEQ) == 0) return c.substring(nameEQ.length, c.length);
    }
    return null;
  }
  function getGet(name) {
    var s = window.location.search;
    s = s.match(new RegExp(name + '=([^&=]+)'));

    var ret = s ? decodeURI(s[1]).replace(/ /g, '_') : false;

    if (!ret && name.indexOf('utm_') === 0) {
      var cookie_name = 'TILDAUTM';
      if (window.location.ancestorOrigins && window.location.ancestorOrigins.length > 0) {
        if (window.location.ancestorOrigins[0] == 'https://ya.zerocoder.ru') {
          cookie_name = 'YA_ZEROCODER_UTM';
        }
      }
      
      try {
        var utm = getCookie(cookie_name);
        utm = decodeURIComponent(utm);
        utm = utm.split('|||');
        for (var n = 0; n < utm.length; n++) {
          var cParameterName = utm[n].split('=');
          var pName = cParameterName[0],
              pValue = cParameterName[1];
          if (pName === name) {
            ret = pValue;
          }
        }
      } catch (e) {
        console.error(e);
      }
    }

    return ret;
  }
